drop table if exists simulative.abonent;
drop table if exists simulative.revenue;
drop table if exists simulative.trafic; 

drop schema if exists simulative;

create schema if not exists simulative;

create table if not exists simulative.abonent (
  ym text, 
  branch text,
  region text,
  segment text, 
  amount int
);
  
create table if not exists simulative.revenue (
  ym text, 
  branch text,
  segment text, 
  revenue float
);

create table if not exists simulative.trafic (
  branch text, 
  segment text, 
  gadget text,
  tarif text, 
  charges float, 
  trafic float
)
